Ex.1

$V_{A}$
$E=10V$
$R=10Ω$
$j$

1 Nodes
2 Reference Node $V_{0}=0V$
$U_{V}=V_{B}-VD=V_{B}$
Resistanceless branch
$V_{C}=V_{D}+60V=\underline{60V}$
3 Nodal equasions:
we switch off sources

Ⓐ $V_{A}\left( \frac{1}{250}+\frac{1}{100}+\frac{1}{200}+\overbrace{ \frac{1}{\infty} }^{ 0 } \right)-\overbrace{ V_{D} }^{ =0V }\cancel{ \left( \frac{1}{250}+0 \right) }-V_{B}\left( \frac{1}{100}+\frac{1}{200} \right)=$
Equvalent branch current $=0+0.6+0+0.5$
Ⓑ $V_{B}\left( \frac{1}{200}+\frac{1}{100}+\frac{1}{50}+0 \right)-V_{A}\left( \frac{1}{100}+\frac{1}{200} \right)-\overbrace{ V_{C} }^{ =60V }\left( \frac{1}{50}+0 \right)$
$=-0.5+0+0.5-1.2$
mulitply everything by 1000
$V_{A}(4+10+5)-V_{B}(10+5)=1100$
$V_{B}(5+10+20)-V_{A}(10+5)-60(20)=-1200$

$$
\begin{cases}
19V_{A}-15V_{B}=1100 \\
-15V_{A}+35V_{B}=0 \ /:(-15)
\end{cases}
$$
$\underline{V_{A}}=\frac{35}{15}V_{B}=\underline{\frac{7}{3}V_{B}}$
$\underbrace{ 19·\frac{7}{3}V_{B}-15V_{B} }_{ 29.33V_{B} }=1100$
$\underline{V_{B}=37.5V}$
if we use Volt Ams and Ohms the result is in Volts

$V_{B}=0V$ (Reference node)
$\underline{V_{A}}=V_{B}+E=E=\underline{30V}$
$I_{A}=\frac{V_{D}-V_{C}}{R_{A}}$
$V_{C}\left( \frac{1}{R}+\frac{1}{0.5R}+\frac{1}{R_{A}}\right)-V_{A}\left( \frac{1}{R} \right)-V_{D}\left( \frac{1}{R_{A}} \right)=0+0+0$$V_{D}\left( \frac{1}{4R}+\frac{1}{R_{A}}+\frac{1}{R} \right)-V_{A}\left( \frac{1}{4R} \right)-V_{C}\left( \frac{1}{R_{A}} \right)=0+0+0$
$V_{C}\left( \frac{1}{10}+\frac{1}{5}+\frac{1}{5} \right)-30\left( \frac{1}{10} \right)-V_{D}\left( \frac{1}{5} \right)=0$
$V_{D}\left( \frac{1}{40}+\frac{1}{5}+\frac{1}{10} \right)-30\left( \frac{1}{40} \right)-V_{C}\left( \frac{1}{5} \right)=0$
$$
\begin{align}
 & \begin{cases}
 V_{C}\left( \frac{1}{10}+\frac{1}{5}+\frac{1}{5} \right)-30\left( \frac{1}{10} \right)-V_{D}\left( \frac{1}{5} \right)=0 \\
V_{D}\left( \frac{1}{40}+\frac{1}{5}+\frac{1}{10} \right)-30\left( \frac{1}{40} \right)-V_{C}\left( \frac{1}{5} \right)=0
\end{cases} \\ \\

 & \begin{cases}
5V_{C}-30-2V_{D}=0 \\
13V_{D}-30-8V_{C}=0
\end{cases} \\ \\
 & \begin{cases}
5V_{C}-2V_{D}=30 \to V_{D}=\frac{5V_{C}-30}{2}=2.5V_{C}-15 \\
13V_{D}-8V_{C}=30
\end{cases} \\ \\
 & 13(2.5V_{C}-15)-8V_{C}=30 \\
 & 32.5V_{C}-195-8V_{C}=30 \\
 & 24.5V_{C}=225 \\
 & V_{C}=9.18V  \\
 \\
 & V_{D}=2.5·9.18=7.95V
\end{align}
$$

$I_{A}=\frac{V_{D}-V_{C}}{R_{A}}=\frac{7.95V-9.18V}{5Ω}=-0.25A=-250mA$
